## 增量升级(v2.3.3->v2.4.0)


### 程序发布前执行项


#### 1、Apollo配置


###### 1.1 LCP-APP


独立部署域 忽略该配置

```
elasticsearch.tenantIds=d037ea10-7ece-49b4-bcba-313ecd4230d6,c9a8ac72-483a-44c5-892e-74428e7010c3,c518f53d-b405-4111-afe1-5c082b284971,43a24eee-3294-40f2-b34d-6aa4c53a9084
```


###### 1.2 CSB-LEGOX


独立部署域 忽略该配置

```
feign.okhttp.readTimeout = 30
feign.okhttp.connectTimeout = 30
```


#### 2、Nacos配置


#### 3、数据库脚本

##### 配置库


###### lcp-app


```

--天舟云默认租户flyway会自动执行，不要手动
--业务域独立部署flyway会自动执行,不要手动
ALTER TABLE state_machine_task ADD app_id varchar(100) NULL;
COMMENT ON COLUMN state_machine_task.app_id IS '应用id';

update state_machine_task t set app_id = oc.app_id from obj_class oc where oc.id  = t.biz_type and t.app_id is null;


CREATE TABLE obj_excel (
       id varchar(64) NOT NULL,
       class_id varchar(64) NULL,
       biz_type varchar(64) NULL,
       template_desc text NULL,
       is_deleted varchar(1) NULL,
       crt_user varchar(32) NULL,
       crt_name varchar(50) NULL,
       crt_time timestamp NULL,
       crt_host varchar(50) NULL,
       upd_user varchar(32) NULL,
       upd_name varchar(50) NULL,
       upd_time timestamp NULL,
       upd_host varchar(50) NULL,
       CONSTRAINT obj_excel_pkey PRIMARY KEY (id)
);

COMMENT ON COLUMN obj_excel.class_id IS '表单标识(分类id)';
COMMENT ON COLUMN obj_excel.biz_type IS '业务类型(import:导入,export:导出)';
COMMENT ON COLUMN obj_excel.template_desc IS '描述信息(导入时:模板说明)';

ALTER TABLE obj_excel_column ADD is_required varchar(1) NULL;
COMMENT ON COLUMN obj_excel_column.is_required IS '必填("1","0")';
ALTER TABLE obj_excel_column ADD sample_data varchar(2000) NULL;
COMMENT ON COLUMN obj_excel_column.sample_data IS '示例数据';

--天舟云默认租户flyway会自动执行，不要手动
--业务域独立部署flyway会自动执行,不要手动
INSERT INTO obj_frontend_plugin (id, name, code, is_inbuilt, repository_code,
                                 library_code, apply_type, is_upload, crt_type,
                                 is_enabled, is_deleted)
VALUES ('9', '历史记录', 'HISTORY', '1', 'tz-render', 'ObjcetHistory', 'TAB', '0', 'LOCAL', '1', '0');
INSERT INTO obj_frontend_plugin_limit (id, plugin_id, relation_type, relation_id, is_enabled, is_deleted)
VALUES (replace(gen_random_uuid()::varchar, '-', ''), '9', 'FORM_TYPE', 'FORM_DATA_OBJ', '1', '0');
INSERT INTO obj_frontend_plugin_limit (id, plugin_id, relation_type, relation_id, is_enabled, is_deleted)
VALUES (replace(gen_random_uuid()::varchar, '-', ''), '9', 'FORM_TYPE', 'FORM_CHANGE', '1', '0');
```


###### lcp-kits 套件服务-公式计算


- 表结构定义语句


```
--天舟云默认租户flyway会自动执行，不要手动
--业务域独立部署flyway会自动执行,不要手动

-- 信息集函数关联关系
CREATE TABLE tp_formula_relation
(
    id              varchar(36)  NOT NULL  PRIMARY KEY,
    c_formula_id    varchar(100) NOT NULL,
    c_relation_type varchar(100) NOT NULL,
    c_relation_id   varchar(100) NOT NULL,
    is_deleted      varchar(4),
    is_enabled      varchar(4),
    crt_user        varchar(64),
    crt_name        varchar(64),
    crt_time        timestamp,
    crt_host        varchar(64),
    upd_user        varchar(64),
    upd_name        varchar(64),
    upd_time        timestamp,
    upd_host        varchar(64),
    tenant_id       varchar(64)
);

COMMENT ON TABLE tp_formula_relation IS '公式关联关系';
COMMENT ON COLUMN tp_formula_relation.id IS '主键';
COMMENT ON COLUMN tp_formula_relation.c_formula_id IS '字段名称';
COMMENT ON COLUMN tp_formula_relation.c_relation_type IS '数据类型';
COMMENT ON COLUMN tp_formula_relation.c_relation_id IS '操作符';
COMMENT ON COLUMN tp_formula_relation.is_deleted IS '是否删除';

CREATE INDEX tp_formula_relation_idx1 ON tp_formula_relation (c_relation_id);
CREATE INDEX tp_formula_relation_idx2 ON tp_formula_relation (c_formula_id);

CREATE TABLE tp_formula
(
    id              varchar(36)  NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY,
    c_trans_content     varchar(2000) NOT NULL,
    c_content       varchar(4000) NOT NULL,
    is_deleted      varchar(4),
    is_enabled      varchar(4),
    crt_user        varchar(64),
    crt_name        varchar(64),
    crt_time        timestamp,
    crt_host        varchar(64),
    upd_user        varchar(64),
    upd_name        varchar(64),
    upd_time        timestamp,
    upd_host        varchar(64),
    tenant_id       varchar(64)
);

COMMENT ON TABLE tp_formula IS '公式冗余表';
COMMENT ON COLUMN tp_formula.id IS '主键';
COMMENT ON COLUMN tp_formula.c_content IS '公式内容';
COMMENT ON COLUMN tp_formula.c_trans_content IS '公式中文翻译';

```

###### 行按钮权限初始化


```
--执行以下 sql，然后复制生成的 sql，在数据库中执行
WITH selected_ids AS (
SELECT id FROM obj_permission_policy WHERE is_create_status = '0' AND description = '默认查看所有单据权限'
)
SELECT 'INSERT INTO obj_permission_object (id, policy_id, object_type, object_id, permission_type, permission_value) VALUES (''' || replace(cast(gen_random_uuid() as VARCHAR), '-', '') || ''', ''' || selected_ids.id || ''',''action'',''TABLE_EDIT_BUTTON'',''visible'',''1'');' FROM selected_ids;

```


如果有报：function gen_random_uuid() does not exist 问题，联系运维黄伟杰 开权限

供应链: 93caaf4e-478e-4026-a87d-e68b0a9d7713

```
update  lcp_page_components  set tenant_id ='93caaf4e-478e-4026-a87d-e68b0a9d7713';
update  component  set tenant_id ='93caaf4e-478e-4026-a87d-e68b0a9d7713';
```

5)、业务组件更新”是否系统组件”字段值为’0’

```
update lcp_page_components set is_sys='0' where is_sys is null;
```
